# Scientific Agent Master Paper List

> Last updated: 2026-07-04
> Current pool built from the Shanghai AI Lab seed survey, high-impact journal entry points, and citation-graph expansion.
> Current status counts: `candidate 0`, `to_read 447`, `background_only 371`, `excluded 53`, `needs_review 0`.
> Confirmed included-and-classified count: `447`.
> This file is the canonical control panel for literature collection, screening, classification, and note coverage.
> Seed survey anchor: `From AI for Science to Agentic Science: A Survey on Autonomous Scientific Discovery` (arXiv:2508.14111v1).
> Annotation schema: `paper_note_templates_and_prompts/ASD_annotation_schema.md`.
> Schema migration note: the current row table still uses legacy filing fields (`Main class`, `Secondary class`, `Tertiary class`). Under the current policy, `01�C11` are the formal scientific-object modules, a paper may eventually carry one or more concrete-object modules, and `01.04` is a separate general-method bucket rather than a formal main class. Full row-level schema migration is still pending.
> Transitional counting rule: historical reaudit filenames still retain `451`, but after duplicate-lineage reconciliation the current active confirmed-core unique-work count is `447`. The stable confirmed count should be computed from records whose `Inclusion status` is `to_read` or `included` and that either have at least one `scientific_object_modules` entry or are explicitly marked in the `01.04` general-method bucket.

## Scope

This master list tracks Agent papers for the Autonomous Scientific Discovery review. Papers are screened under the project Agent-inclusion criteria, then classified by scientific research object into the formal `01-11` scientific-object module system, with multi-module assignment allowed when a paper contains identifiable experiments, validations, benchmark tasks, case studies, or reported results for multiple concrete scientific objects, plus the separate `01.04` general-method bucket for papers without any concrete scientific-object experiments, validations, benchmark tasks, case studies, or reported results. Status values such as `candidate`, `background_only`, `excluded`, and `needs_review` remain in the list so decisions are not re-litigated later. Historical reaudit filenames still retain `451`, but the current active confirmed-core unique-work count after duplicate-lineage reconciliation is `447`.
